  2. I've used this electric shaver for over a month now, and I find it to be much less irritating to my skin than a blade+shaving cream. For those with sensitive skin, I definitely recommend making the switch to electric, plus this Braun automatically cleans itself so you won't have weird stuff growing inside the shaver!<br /><br />It took a little bit of practice to get the closest shave possible--I found it helps to go over the skin a little slower to ensure good contact with the stubble. You also need to vary the angle of approach around your face to make sure there's a 90 degree angle with the shaver. There is a three position sensitivity setting, for me the most rigid setting worked better to get a close shave and it wasn't irritating to my face. The included trimmer is great for sideburns.<br /><br />This shaver is fantastic for 95% of my face... but it has trouble giving a close shave on my neck around the windpipe. So far that's the only drawback to this shaver. The circular head shavers may be a little better getting those tough spots on the neck, but for me this model is much less irritating to the skin overall, and maintenance is very easy.

The neck and jaw line I have noticed will have a little more stubble left over (why 4 stars) but the irritation-to-closeness of shave ratio is definitely in the positive. This review might have to be edited after I get past my first three weeks but I am happy right now.<br /><br />Clean and Storage: 4.5 stars<br />Cleaning this shaver is extremely easy. Stick it in the clean and charge station and hit start. It does the work for you. Plus it lubricates the shaver for you as well. One thing to keep in mind is that the shaver air dries after the cleaning so if you need to shave right away after cleaning you will have problems. I have not had any issues as time between shaving for me is usually 20 or more hours. Even if I shaved in the morning and needed a touch up at night I don't think there would be any issue. The shaver can be stored right in the cleaning station so that is good and it look nice with a pleasant blue color given off. Makes a nice night light for the occasional bathroom visit during the night. The only complaint I would have is that the AC/DC converter is quite long. This might fit under the design heading better but if you are like me and keep this on your bathroom counter for storage you will have a larger plug converter hanging out. Not a huge deal but for people that want a more clean look while not in use can be a issue.<br /><br />Overall: 4.5 stars<br />Amazon does not allow half stars so 4 is what I rated this. I would recommend this shaver to all of my friends. While it might be a little expensive then some of the options out there it gets the job done well and comfortably. I would defiantly suggest spending a little more on a quality shaver then a cheap solution that eats up your face. This is a foil shaver so if you like rotary shavers more this would not be for you but everyone else should check this out.t over (why 4 stars) but the irritation-to-closeness of shave ratio is definitely in the positive. Now, if it will just last as long...<br /><br />David<br /><br />edit 5/9/12: I think the 'clean and renew' system is a bit over-hyped, and there are a lot of ways to keep the shaver cleaned, and lubricated, if lubricating is actually necessary. And one of the 'manual' ways suggested by Braun will, and I know this from experience, greatly reduce the useful life of the mesh screen...that of loosening the head of the shaver, and then running it to shake out the clippings. Much better ways exist, including removing the head and tapping it on a hard surface, and brushing out the cutter bar with the brush and then running the shaver and blowing on it. And a favorite way of mine is to keep a bottle of 'canned air' on hand, and literally 'blowing' it clean. This works very, very well, and gets out the dust from places the brush cannot reach.   473. I've been using this for a week straight now (7 days of shaving). What can I say, it is great. Everything arrived packaged very nicely. The cleaning station is simple enough to get set up. I've been shaving for 14 years using some form of manual razor, with a dabble of cheaper electric brands for going to the field. I have to say that this thing shaves just as close as shaving against the grain with a 3-5 blade manual razor. I am very impressed with the quality of shave. Not to mention, it is super convenient. It glides across my face. Every other electric razor I've tried seems like complete garbage compared to this thing. I had a hard time choosing between this and the 3 series, but I think I made the right choice. Here are my only two &#34;complaints&#34;:<br /><br />1- The pivoting head doesn't really pivot too much while I use it. I have the adjuster set to the &#34;free pivot&#34; notch, and it does pivot in my fingers, but not a whole lot on my face. Granted, this has not had any effect whatsoever on the comfort or quality of the shave just an interesting note.<br /><br />2- The cleaning station didn't want to clean one time when I pressed the button. I simply unplugged it and plugged it back in and it was good to go and no problems since.<br /><br />Final note - I remember reading something about the cleaning station not letting you charge without cleaning (don't remember if it was a 3 or 5 series review), this station does allow the razor to be charged without committing to the cleaning process.
